\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00456}00456 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Computes the plane given three points(clockwise).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00457}00457 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00458}00458 \textcolor{comment}{            * Calculates the plane given three points(clockwise) by taking the perpendicular vector that would intersect}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00459}00459 \textcolor{comment}{            * a triangle that the three points represent. The plane is defined as a normal and distance from the origin.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00460}00460 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00461}00461 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur when the given plane's position points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00462}00462 \textcolor{comment}{            * are collinear.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00463}00463 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00464}00464 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_planePositionA The plane position a.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00489}00489 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00490}00490 \textcolor{comment}{            * Tests whether a point is contained within a polygon by counting how many times a line that extends to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00494}00494 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point is not contained within the polygon, the out result is 0.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00496}00496 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur if the pointer to the polygon's points}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00578}00578 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Computes the closest point on a sphere's surface to a point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00579}00579 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00580}00580 \textcolor{comment}{            * Computes the closest point on a sphere's surface to a point by getting the normalized direction of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00581}00581 \textcolor{comment}{            * sphere's center to the given point and scaling that by the sphere's radius.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00582}00582 \textcolor{comment}{            * The out point is the result of this computation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00583}00583 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00584}00584 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur if the query point is the sphere's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00585}00585 \textcolor{comment}{            * center which results an infinite amount of valid results that cannot be represented in a single out point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00586}00586 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00587}00587 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_sphere     The sphere.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00588}00588 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_queryPoint The query point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00589}00589 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outPoint   The out point that lies on the sphere's surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00590}00590 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00591}00591 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::FAILURE The calculation failed.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00714}00714 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a point to triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00715}00715 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00716}00716 \textcolor{comment}{            * Tests a point to a triangle by checking if the point lies on the surface plane of the triangle's normal and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00717}00717 \textcolor{comment}{            * then if the barycentric coordinate's are all positive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00718}00718 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point lies on the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00719}00719 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point does not lie on the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00720}00720 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00721}00721 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00722}00722 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur if the triangle is degenerate.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00723}00723 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00724}00724 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_point          The point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00725}00725 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_triangle       The triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00726}00726 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outResult      The out result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00727}00727 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outBarycentric If non-\/null, the out barycentric coordinates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00728}00728 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00729}00729 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::FAILURE The calculation failed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00730}00730 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::SUCCESS The calculation succeeded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00731}00731 \textcolor{comment}{            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00732}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_ac3788887e3d6e740f4073e7dabcc93a8}{00732}}             \textcolor{keyword}{static} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{GReturn}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_ac3788887e3d6e740f4073e7dabcc93a8}{TestPointToTriangleF}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{MATH::GVECTORF}} \_point, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_f}{MATH::GTRIANGLEF}} \_triangle, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{GCollisionCheck}}\& \_outResult, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{MATH::GVECTORF}}* \_outBarycentric) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_ggaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617a741d913c61ad067adf01a85e6807ad21}{GReturn::NO\_IMPLEMENTATION}}; \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00734}00734 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a point to a plane.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00735}00735 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00736}00736 \textcolor{comment}{            * Tests a point to a plane by dotting the point and the plane's surface direction and then subtracting the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00737}00737 \textcolor{comment}{            * plane's distance from the result of that dot product.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00738}00738 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point lies on the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00739}00739 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point lies below the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::BELOW.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00740}00740 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point lies above the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::ABOVE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00741}00741 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00742}00742 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_point      The point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00743}00743 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_plane      The plane.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l00839}00839 \textcolor{comment}{            * detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line's start}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01022}01022 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a triangle to a triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01023}01023 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01025}01025 \textcolor{comment}{            * other triangle's face and then brings the triangles into canonical form to check if any of the edges of one}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01336}01336 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Tests OBB to OBB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01337}01337 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01338}01338 \textcolor{comment}{            * Tests if a collision exists between OBB to OBB by checking if the sum of their projected radii is less}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01339}01339 \textcolor{comment}{            * than the distance between their projected centers meaning a separating axis exists. The result will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01340}01340 \textcolor{comment}{            * stored in \_outResult as either GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION or GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01341}01341 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the OBBs contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01342}01342 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the OBBs don't contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01343}01343 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01352}01352 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Intersect line to triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01353}01353 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01354}01354 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a line to a clockwise triangle by computing if the line pierces the triangle. A collision will only be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01355}01355 \textcolor{comment}{            * detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line's start}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01356}01356 \textcolor{comment}{            * point lies in front of the triangle and the line's end lies in back of the triangle). Provides the point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01357}01357 \textcolor{comment}{            * of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01358}01358 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line contacts the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01359}01359 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line does not contact the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01360}01360 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01361}01361 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01532}01532 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Intersect ray to capsule.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01533}01533 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01534}01534 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a ray to a capsule by computing the closest points on the ray's path to the capsule's center line and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01535}01535 \textcolor{comment}{            * reduces the query to a point to sphere test. Provides the point of contact along with the interval the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01536}01536 \textcolor{comment}{            * contact occurs on the ray.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01537}01537 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the ray's path contacts the capsule, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01538}01538 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the ray's path does not contact the capsule, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01731}01731 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Intersect AABB to AABB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01732}01732 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01733}01733 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test an AABB to an AABB by checking if they overlap on all three axes. Provides the minimal translation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01734}01734 \textcolor{comment}{            * information: two points on each shape's surface,the direction the two points form, and distance required to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01735}01735 \textcolor{comment}{            * translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01736}01736 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the AABBs contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01737}01737 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the AABBs don't contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01738}01738 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01739}01739 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_aabb1          The first aabb.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01740}01740 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_aabb2          The second aabb.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01741}01741 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outResult      The out result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01742}01742 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outContactAABB The out contact a bb.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01743}01743 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outDirection   The out direction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01744}01744 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outDistance    The out distance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01745}01745 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01746}01746 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::SUCCESS The calculation succeeded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01747}01747 \textcolor{comment}{            */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01942}01942 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Tests whether a point lies within a polygon or not.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01943}01943 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01944}01944 \textcolor{comment}{            * Tests whether a point is contained within a polygon by counting how many times a line that extends to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01945}01945 \textcolor{comment}{            * infinity intersects the sides of the polygon.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01946}01946 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point is contained within the polygon, the out result is 1. This does not include the polygon's}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01948}01948 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point is not contained within the polygon, the out result is 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01949}01949 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01950}01950 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur if the pointer to the polygon's points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01951}01951 \textcolor{comment}{            * is null or if the point count is less than 3.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l01952}01952 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02032}02032 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Computes the closest point on a sphere's surface to a point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02033}02033 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02034}02034 \textcolor{comment}{            * Computes the closest point on a sphere's surface to a point by getting the normalized direction of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02035}02035 \textcolor{comment}{            * sphere's center to the given point and scaling that by the sphere's radius.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02036}02036 \textcolor{comment}{            * The out point is the result of this computation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02037}02037 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02038}02038 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur if the query point is the sphere's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02039}02039 \textcolor{comment}{            * center which results an infinite amount of valid results that cannot be represented in a single out point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02040}02040 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02041}02041 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_sphere     The sphere.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02042}02042 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_queryPoint The query point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02043}02043 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outPoint   The out point that lies on the sphere's surface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02044}02044 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02045}02045 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::FAILURE The calculation failed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02046}02046 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::SUCCESS The calculation succeeded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02047}02047 \textcolor{comment}{            */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02051}02051 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02052}02052 \textcolor{comment}{            * Computes the closest point on a capsule's surface to a point by finding the closest point to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02053}02053 \textcolor{comment}{            * capsule's center line and then computing the closest point to a sphere.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02055}02055 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02057}02057 \textcolor{comment}{            * center line which results an infinite amount of valid results that cannot be represented in a single out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02058}02058 \textcolor{comment}{            * point.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02168}02168 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a point to triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02169}02169 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02170}02170 \textcolor{comment}{            * Tests a point to a triangle by checking if the point lies on the surface plane of the triangle's normal and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02171}02171 \textcolor{comment}{            * then if the barycentric coordinate's are all positive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02172}02172 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point lies on the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02173}02173 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point does not lie on the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02174}02174 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02175}02175 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02176}02176 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur if the triangle is degenerate.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02177}02177 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02178}02178 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_point          The point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02179}02179 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_triangle       The triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02180}02180 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outResult      The out result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02181}02181 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outBarycentric If non-\/null, the out barycentric coordinates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02182}02182 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02183}02183 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::FAILURE The calculation failed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02184}02184 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::SUCCESS The calculation succeeded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02185}02185 \textcolor{comment}{            */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02188}02188 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a point to a plane.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02189}02189 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02190}02190 \textcolor{comment}{            * Tests a point to a plane by dotting the point and the plane's surface direction and then subtracting the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02191}02191 \textcolor{comment}{            * plane's distance from the result of that dot product.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02192}02192 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point lies on the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02193}02193 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point lies below the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::BELOW.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02194}02194 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the point lies above the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::ABOVE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02195}02195 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02196}02196 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_point      The point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02197}02197 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_plane      The plane.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02198}02198 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outResult  The out result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02199}02199 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02200}02200 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::SUCCESS The calculation succeeded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02201}02201 \textcolor{comment}{            */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02290}02290 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a line to a triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02291}02291 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02292}02292 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a line to a clockwise triangle by computing if the line pierces the triangle. A collision will only be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02293}02293 \textcolor{comment}{            * detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line's start}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02294}02294 \textcolor{comment}{            * point lies in front of the triangle and the line's end lies in back of the triangle).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02295}02295 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line contacts the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02296}02296 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line does not contact the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02297}02297 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02298}02298 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02299}02299 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_line           The line.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02301}02301 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outResult      The out result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02302}02302 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outBarycentric If non-\/null, the out barycentric.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02303}02303 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02398}02398 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a ray to a plane.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02399}02399 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02400}02400 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a ray to a plane by computing if the ray's path pierces the plane.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02401}02401 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the ray contacts the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02404}02404 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the ray lies above the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::ABOVE.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02476}02476 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a triangle to a triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02477}02477 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02481}02481 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the triangle's contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02492}02492 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Test a triangle to a plane.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02493}02493 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02494}02494 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a triangle to a plane to compute if all of the triangle's vertices lie completely on one side of the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02603}02603 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02604}02604 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a plane to a capsule by computing the closest points on the plane to the capsule's start and end points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02605}02605 \textcolor{comment}{            * and then perform a line to capsule test.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02606}02606 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the plane contacts the capsule, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02607}02607 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the capsule lies below the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::BELOW.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02608}02608 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the capsule lies above the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::ABOVE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02609}02609 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02610}02610 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_plane      The plane.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02611}02611 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_capsule    The capsule.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02612}02612 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outResult  The out result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02613}02613 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02614}02614 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::FAILURE The calculation failed.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02791}02791 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Tests OBB to OBB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02792}02792 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02793}02793 \textcolor{comment}{            * Tests if a collision exists between OBB to OBB by checking if the sum of their projected radii is less}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02794}02794 \textcolor{comment}{            * than the distance between their projected centers meaning a separating axis exists. The result will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02795}02795 \textcolor{comment}{            * stored in \_outResult as either GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION or GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02796}02796 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the OBBs contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02797}02797 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the OBBs don't contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02798}02798 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02799}02799 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_obb1       The first OBB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02800}02800 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_obb2       The second OBB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02801}02801 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outResult  The out result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02802}02802 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02807}02807 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Intersect line to triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02808}02808 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02809}02809 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a line to a clockwise triangle by computing if the line pierces the triangle. A collision will only be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02810}02810 \textcolor{comment}{            * detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line's start}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02811}02811 \textcolor{comment}{            * point lies in front of the triangle and the line's end lies in back of the triangle). Provides the point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02812}02812 \textcolor{comment}{            * of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02813}02813 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line contacts the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02814}02814 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line does not contact the triangle, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02815}02815 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02816}02816 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02817}02817 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_line               The line.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02818}02818 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_triangle           The triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02819}02819 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outResult          The out result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02820}02820 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outContactPoint    The out contact point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02821}02821 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outBarycentric     If non-\/null, the out barycentric.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02822}02822 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outDirection       The out direction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02823}02823 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outInterval        The out interval along the direction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02824}02824 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02830}02830 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02831}02831 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a line to a plane by computing the interval along the line that intersects the plane. Provides the point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02832}02832 \textcolor{comment}{            * of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02833}02833 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line contacts the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02834}02834 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line is coplanar to the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02835}02835 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line lies below the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::BELOW.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l02836}02836 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the line lies above the plane, the out result is GCollisionCheck::ABOVE.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03047}03047 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the spheres do not contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03125}03125 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03126}03126 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a capsule to another capsule by computing the closest points on each capsule's center line and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03127}03127 \textcolor{comment}{            * performing a sphere to sphere test. Provides the minimal translation information: two points on each shape's surface,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03128}03128 \textcolor{comment}{            * the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03130}03130 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the capsules contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03131}03131 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the capsules don't contact, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03132}03132 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03133}03133 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_capsule1           The first capsule.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03147}03147 \textcolor{comment}{            * Test a capsule to an AABB by increasing the AABB's extents by the capsule's radius and then performing a}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03152}03152 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the capsule does not contact the AABB, the out result is GCollisionCheck::NO\_COLLISION.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03304}03304 \textcolor{comment}{            //! Compute the barycentric coordinates of a point to triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03305}03305 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{comment}{            /*!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03306}03306 \textcolor{comment}{            * Compute the barycentric coordinates given three points of a triangle with a point in respect to that triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03307}03307 \textcolor{comment}{            * Both triangle and point must be coplanar. The result is stored in a vector representing the barycentric coords.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03308}03308 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03309}03309 \textcolor{comment}{            * If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur when the triangle is degenerate.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03310}03310 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03311}03311 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_a              The first point of a triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03312}03312 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_b              The second point of a triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03313}03313 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_c              The third point of a triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03314}03314 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [in]   \_p              The point coplanar with the triangle points.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03315}03315 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)param [out]  \_outBarycentric The out barycentric coordinates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03316}03316 \textcolor{comment}{            *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03317}03317 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::FAILURE The calculation failed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03318}03318 \textcolor{comment}{            * \(\backslash\)retval GReturn::SUCCESS The calculation succeeded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_g_collision_8h_source_l03319}03319 \textcolor{comment}{            */}}
